Mahāparinirvāṇasūtra

Wal 1.1 evaṃ mayā śrutam ||

Wal 1.2 ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavān rājagṛhe viharati gṛdhrakūṭe parvate || tena khalu samayena rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro vṛjibhiḥ sārdhaṃ prativiruddhaḥ ||

Wal 1.3 sa evaṃ pariṣadi vācaṃ bhāṣate || aham imān vṛjīn ṛddhāṃś ca sphītāṃś ca kṣemāṃś ca subhikṣāṃś cākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṃś cotsādayiṣyāmi vināśayiṣyāmy anayena vyasanam āpādayiṣyāmi ||

Wal 1.4 atha rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro varṣākāraṃ brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātram āmantrayate ||

Wal 1.5 ehi tvaṃ varṣākāra yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkrama || upetyāsmākaṃ vacanena bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vandasvālpābādhatāṃ ca pṛcchālpātaṅkatāṃ ca laghūtthānatāṃ ca yātrāṃ ca balaṃ ca sukhaṃ cānavadyatāṃ ca sparśavihāratāṃ ca ||

Wal 1.6 evaṃ ca vada || rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro vṛjibhiḥ sārdhaṃ prativiruddhaḥ || sa evaṃ pariṣadi vācaṃ bhāṣate || aham imān vṛjīn ṛddhāṃś ca sphītāṃś ca kṣemāṃś ca subhikṣāṃś cākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṃś cotsādayiṣyāmi vināśayiṣyāmy anayena vyasanam āpādayiṣyāmi ||

Wal 1.7 kiṃ bhagavān āmantrayate || yathā varṣākāra sa bhagavāṃ vyākaroti tathaivodgṛhāṇa || tat kasmād dhetoḥ || avitathāvādino hi bhavanti tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ ||

Wal 1.8 evaṃ deveti varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro rājño māgadhasyājātaśatror vaidehīputrasya pratiśrutya sarvaśvetaṃ vaḍabāratham abhiruhya … māṇavagaṇaparivṛtaḥ sauvarṇena daṇḍakama … rājagṛhān niryāti bhagavato ’ntikenopadarśanāya bhagavantaṃ paryupāsanāyai || tasya yāvad yānasya bhūmis tāvad yānena gatvā yānād avatīrya padbhyām eva gṛdhrakūṭaṃ parvatam abhiruhya yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagāmopetya bhagavatā sārdhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ saṃmodanīṃ saṃraṃjanīṃ vividhāṃ kathāṃ vyatisāryaikānte nyaṣīdat |

Wal 1.9 ekānte niṣaṇṇo varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamāhāmātro bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 1.10 rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vandaty alpābādhatāṃ ca pṛcchaty alpātaṅkatāṃ ca pūrvavad yāvat sparśavihāratāṃ ca ||

Wal 1.11 sukhī bhavatu varṣākāra rājā māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputras tvaṃ ca ||

Wal 1.12 rājā bhadanta māgadho ’jātaśatrur vaidehīputro vṛjibhiḥ sārdhaṃ prativiruddhaḥ || sa evaṃ pariṣadi vācaṃ bhāṣate || aham imān vṛjīn ṛddhāṃś ca sphītāṃś ca kṣemāṃś ca subhikṣāṃś cākīrṇabahujanamanuṣyāṃś cotsādayiṣyāmi vināśayiṣyāmy anayena vyasanam āpādayiṣyāmi ||

Wal 1.13 kiṃ bhagavāṅ gautama āmantrayate ||

Wal 1.14 ekam ahaṃ varṣākāra samayaṃ vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu viharāmi cāpāle caitye || tatra mayā vṛjīnāṃ saptāparihāṇīyā dharmā deśitāḥ || yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjaya imān saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante vṛjiṣu ca saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.15 evam ahaṃ bhadantāsya bhagavato gautamasya saṃkṣiptena bhāṣitasyāvibhaktasya vistareṇārthaṃ nājānāmi || bhagavān gautamo saṃkṣiptena bhāṣitasyārthaṃ vibhaktaṃ vistareṇa bhāṣeta || evam ahaṃ bhagavato gautamasya saṃkṣiptena bhāṣitasyāvibhaktaṃ vistareṇārthaṃ sādhu evājñāsyāmi ||

Wal 1.16 tena khalu samayenāyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ sthito bhagavantaṃ vījayamānaḥ || tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 1.17 kiṃ nu tvayānanda śrutaṃ vṛjayo ’bhīkṣṇasannipātā abhīkṣṇaṃ sannipātabahulā viharanti ||

Wal 1.18 śrutaṃ me bhadanta vṛjayo ’bhīkṣṇasannipātā abhīkṣṇaṃ sannipātabahulā viharanti ||

Wal 1.19 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo ’bhīkṣṇasannipātā abhīkṣṇaṃ sannipātabahulā vihariṣyanti vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.20 kiṃ nu tvayānanda śrutaṃ vṛjayaḥ samagrāḥ sannipatanti samagrā vyuttiṣṭhanti samagrā vṛjikaraṇīyāni kurvanti ||

Wal 1.21 śrutaṃ me bhadanta vṛjayaḥ samagrāḥ sannipatanti samagrā vyuttiṣṭhanti samagrā vṛjikaraṇīyāni kurvanti ||

Wal 1.22 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayaḥ samagrāḥ sannipatiṣyanti samagrā vyutthāsyanti samagrā vṛjikaraṇīyāni kariṣyanti vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.23 kiṃ nu tvayānanda śrutaṃ vṛjayo ’praṇihitaṃ na praṇidadhati praṇihitaṃ ca na samucchindati yathāprajñaptaṃ vṛjidharmaṃ samādāya vartante ||

Wal 1.24 śrutaṃ me bhadanta vṛjayo ’praṇihitaṃ na praṇidadhati praṇihitaṃ ca na samucchindanti yathāprajñaptaṃ vṛjidharmaṃ samādāya vartante ||

Wal 1.25 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo ’praṇihitaṃ na praṇidhāsyanti praṇihitaṃ ca na samucchetsyanti yathāprajñaptaṃ vṛjidharmaṃ samādāya vartiṣyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.26 kiṃ nu tvayānanda śrutaṃ yās tā vṛjīnāṃ vṛjiprajāpatyo vṛjikumārikāś ca pitṛrakṣitā mātṛrakṣitā bhrātṛrakṣitā bhaginīrakṣitāḥ śvaśurarakṣitā śvaśrurakṣitā jñātirakṣitā gotrarakṣitāḥ saparidaṇḍāḥ sasvāmikāḥ kanyāḥ paraparigṛhītā antaśo mālāguṇaparikṣiptā api tadrūpāsu na sahasā balenānupraskandya kāmeṣu cāritram āpadyante ||

Wal 1.27 śrutaṃ me bhadanta vṛjayo yās tā vṛjīnāṃ vṛjiprajāpatyo vṛjikumārikāś ca pitṛrakṣitā mātṛrakṣitā pūrvavad yāvad antaśo mālāguṇaparikṣiptā api tadrūpāsu na sahasā balenānupraskandya kāmeṣu cāritram āpadyante ||

Wal 1.28 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo yās tā vṛjīnāṃ vṛjiprajāpatyo vṛjikumārikāś ca pūrvavad yāvad antaśo mālāguṇaparikṣiptā api tadrūpāsu na sahasā balenānupraskandya kāmeṣu cāritram āpatsyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.29 kiṃ nu tvayānanda śrutaṃ vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṃ vṛjimahallakās tān satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti teṣāṃ vacanaṃ śrotavyaṃ manyante ||

Wal 1.30 śrutaṃ me bhadanta vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṃ vṛjimahallakās tān satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti teṣāṃ vacanaṃ śrotavyaṃ manyante ||

Wal 1.31 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṃ vṛjimahallakās tān satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti teṣāṃ vacanaṃ śrotavyaṃ maṃsyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.32 kiṃ nu tvayānanda śrutaṃ vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṃ caturdikṣu vṛjicaityās tān satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti teṣāṃ ca paurāṇaṃ cihnavṛttaṃ na samucchindanti ||

Wal 1.33 śrutaṃ me bhadanta vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṃ caturdikṣu vṛjicaityās tān satkurvanti gurukurvanti mānayanti pūjayanti teṣāṃ ca paurāṇaṃ cihnavṛttaṃ na samucchindanti ||

Wal 1.34 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjayo ye te vṛjīnāṃ caturdikṣu vṛjicaityās tān satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti teṣāṃ ca paurāṇaṃ cihnavṛttaṃ na samucchetsyanti vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.35 kiṃ nu tvayānanda śrutaṃ vṛjīnām arhatām antike tīvracetasa ārakṣāsmṛtiḥ pratyupasthitā kaccid anāgatāś cārhanta āgaccheyur āgatāś cābhirameraṃs te ca na vihanyerañ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkāraiḥ ||

Wal 1.36 śrutaṃ me bhadanta vṛjīnām arhatām antike tīvracetasa ārakṣāsmṛtiḥ pratyupasthitā kaccid anāgatāś cārhanta āgaccheyur āgatāś cābhirameraṃs te ca na vihanyerañ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkāraiḥ ||

Wal 1.37 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjīnām arhatām antike tīvracetasa ārakṣāsmṛtiḥ pratyupasthitā bhaviṣyati kaccid anāgatāś cārhanta āgaccheyur āgatāś cābhirameraṃs te ca na vihanyerañ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārair vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.38 yāvac ca varṣākāra vṛjaya imān saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante vṛjiṣu ca saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva vṛjīnāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 1.39

Wal 1.40 ekaikena tāvad bho gautamāṅgena samanvāgatā vṛjayo ’gamanīyāḥ syū rājño māgadhasyājātaśatror vaidehīputrasya kaḥ punar vādaḥ sarvaiḥ ||

Wal 1.41 hanta bho gautama gamiṣyāmo bahukṛtyāḥ smo bahukaraṇīyāḥ ||

Wal 1.42 yasyedānīṃ varṣākāra kālaṃ manyase ||

Wal 1.43 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 2.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate || yāvanto bhikṣavo gṛdhrakūṭaparvatam upaniśritya viharanti tān sarvān upasthānaśālāyāṃ sannipātaya ||

Wal 2.2 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya yāvanto bhikṣavo gṛdhrakūṭaṃ parvatam upaniśritya viharanti tān sarvān upasthānaśālāyāṃ sannipātayitvā yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt || ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 2.3 yāvanto bhadanta bhikṣavo gṛdhrakūṭaṃ parvatam upaniśritya viharanti te sarva upasthānaśālāyāṃ sannipatitāḥ || yasyedānīṃ bhagavāṅ kālaṃ manyate ||

Wal 2.4 atha bhagavān yenopasthānaśālā tenopajagāma || upetya purastād bhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat || niṣadya bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate sma ||

Wal 2.5 saptāhaṃ vo bhikṣavo ’parihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.6 yāvac ca bhikṣavo ’bhīkṣṇasannipātā abhīkṣṇaṃ sannipātabahulā vihariṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.7 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ samagrāḥ sannipatiṣyanti samagrā vyutthāsyanti samagrāḥ saṃghakaraṇīyāni kariṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.8 yāvac ca bhikṣavo ’praṇihitaṃ na praṇidhāsyanti praṇihitaṃ ca na samucchetsyanti yathāprajñaptikāṃ śikṣāṃ samādāya vartiṣyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.9 yāvac ca bhikṣavas tṛṣṇāyāḥ paunarbhavikyā nandirāgasahagatāyās tatra tatrābhinandinyā vaśaṃ na gacchanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.10 yāvac ca bhikṣavo ye te bhikṣavaḥ sthavirā rātrijñāś cirapravrajitā … tān satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti teṣāṃ vacanaṃ śrotavyaṃ maṃsyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.11 yāvac ca bhikṣavo ’raṇyavanaprasthāni prāntāni śayanāsanāny adhyāvasiṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.12 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ sabrahmacāriṇām antike tīvracetasa ārakṣāsmṛtiḥ pratyupasthitā kaccid anāgatāś ca sabrahmacāriṇa āgaccheyur āgatāś cābhirameraṃs te ca na vihanyerañ cīvarapiṇḍapātaśayanāsanaglānapratyayabhaiṣajyapariṣkārair vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.13 yāvac ca bhikṣava imān saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante bhikṣuṣu ca saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.14 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.15 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ śāstāraṃ satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti śāstāraṃ satkṛtvā gurukṛtvā mānayitvā pūjayitvopaśritya vihariṣyanti dharmaṃ śikṣām anuśāsanam apramādaṃ pratisaṃstaraṃ samādhiṃ satkariṣyanti gurukariṣyanti mānayiṣyanti pūjayiṣyanti samādhiṃ satkṛtvā gurukṛtvā mānayitvā pūjayitvopaśritya vihariṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.16 Nur im Tib.

Wal 2.17 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.18 yāvac ca bhikṣavo na karmārāmā bhaviṣyanti na bhāṣyārāmā na nidrārāmā na saṃgaṇikārāmā … viśeṣādhigamenāntarāvasān … vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.19 Nur im Tib.

Wal 2.20 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.21 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ śrāddhā bhaviṣyanti hrīmanto bhaviṣyanty avatrāpiṇa ārabdhavīryā upasthitasmṛtayaḥ samāhitāḥ prajñāvanto bhaviṣyanti vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.22 Nur im Tib.

Wal 2.23 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.24 yāvac ca bhikṣavo dharmajñā arthajñāḥ kālajñā mātrajñā ātmajñāḥ pariṣajjñāḥ pudgalavarāvarajñā vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.25 Nur im Tib.

Wal 2.26 aparān api saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.27 yāvac ca bhikṣavaḥ smṛtisaṃbodhyaṅgaṃ bhāvayiṣyanti vivekaniśritaṃ virāganiśritaṃ nirodhaniśritaṃ vyavasargapariṇataṃ dharmavicayavīryaprītiprasrabdhisamādhyupekṣāsaṃbodhyaṅgaṃ bhāvayiṣyanti vivekaniśritaṃ virāganiśritaṃ nirodhaniśritaṃ vyavasargapariṇataṃ vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.28 yāvac ca bhikṣava imān saptāparihāṇīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante bhikṣuṣu ca saptāparihāṇīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.29 ṣaḍ ahaṃ vo bhikṣavaḥ saṃraṃjanīyān dharmān deśayiṣyāmi tāñ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || ṣaṭ saṃraṃjanīyā dharmāḥ katame ||

Wal 2.30 maitraṃ me kāyakarma pratyupasthitaṃ bhaviṣyati śāstur antike vijñānāñ ca sabrahmacāriṇām || ayaṃ dharmaḥ saṃraṃjanīyaḥ priyakaraṇo gurukaraṇo manāpakaraṇaḥ priyatvāya gurutvāya gauravāya bhāvanāya saṃgrahāya samādhaye ’vigrahāyāvivādāya ekotībhāvāya saṃvartate ||

Wal 2.31 maitraṃ vākkarma

Wal 2.32 maitraṃ manaskarma

Wal 2.33 ye te lābhā dhārmikā dharmalabdhā antataḥ pātragatāḥ pātraparyāpannās tadrūpeṣu lābheṣu sādhāraṇaparibhojino bhaviṣyāmo ’pratiguptabhojinaḥ sārdhaṃ vijñaiḥ sabrahmacāribhiḥ ||

ayaṃ dharmaḥ saṃraṃjanīyaḥ pūrvavat ||

Wal 2.34 yāni tāni śīlāny akhaṇḍāny acchidrāṇy aśabalāny akalmāṣāṇi bhujiṣyāṇy aparāmṛṣṭāni susamāptāni susamādattāni vijñapraśastāny agarhitāni vijñais tadrūpaiḥ śīlaiḥ śīlasāmānyagatā bhaviṣyāmaḥ sārdhaṃ vijñaiḥ sabrahmacāribhiḥ || ayaṃ dharmaḥ saṃraṃjanīyaḥ pūrvavat ||

Wal 2.35 yeyaṃ dṛṣṭir āryā nairyāṇikā nairvedhikā niryāti tatkarasamyagduḥkhakṣayāya duḥkhasyāntakriyāyai tadrūpayā dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭisāmānyagatā bhaviṣyāmaḥ sārdhaṃ vijñaiḥ sabrahmacāribhiḥ || ayaṃ dharmaḥ saṃraṃjanīyaḥ pūrvavad yāvad ekotībhāvāya saṃvartate ||

Wal 2.36 yāvac ca bhikṣava imān ṣaṭ saṃraṃjanīyān dharmān samādāya vartiṣyante bhikṣuṣu ca ṣaṭ saṃraṃjanīyā dharmāḥ sandrakṣyante vṛddhir eva bhikṣūṇāṃ pratikāṃkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ na parihāṇiḥ ||

Wal 2.37 Nur Chin.

Hier im Tib. Uddāna

Wal 3.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate || āgamayānanda yena pāṭaligrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 3.2 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt || atha bhagavān sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena magadheṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caran antarā ca pāṭaligrāmakam antarā ca rājagṛhaṃ rājāgārake rātrīṃ viharati veṇuyaṣṭikām upaniśritya ||

Wal 3.3 atha bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate sma || caturṇāṃ bhikṣava āryasatyānām ajñānād adarśanād anavabodhād aprativedhād idaṃ dīrgham adhvānaṃ saṃdhāvitaṃ saṃsṛtaṃ mayā yuṣmābhir eva ca || katameṣāṃ caturṇām ||

Wal 3.4 duḥkhasya duḥkhasamudayasya duḥkhanirodhasya duḥkhanirodhagāminyāḥ pratipado ’jñānād adarśanād anavabodhād aprativedhād idaṃ dīrgham adhvānaṃ saṃdhāvitaṃ saṃsṛtaṃ mayā yuṣmābhir eva ca ||

Wal 3.5 tad idaṃ duḥkham āryasatyam anuviddhaṃ pratividdham ucchinnā bhavanetrī vikṣīṇo jātisaṃsāro nāstīdānīṃ punarbhavaḥ ||

Wal 3.6 duḥkhasamudayo duḥkhanirodho duḥkhanirodhagāminī pratipad āryasatyam anuviddhaṃ pratividdham ucchinnā bhavanetrī vikṣīṇo jātisaṃsāro nāstīdānīṃ punarbhavaḥ ||

Wal 3.7 Nur im Tib.

Wal 3.8 caturṇām āryasatyānāṃ
yathābhūtam adarśanāt ||

saṃsṛtaṃ dīrgham adhvānaṃ
mayā yuṣmābhir eva ca | 1

Wal 3.9 tāni satyāni dṛṣṭāni
bhavanetrī samuddhṛtā ||

vikṣīṇo jātisaṃsāro
nāstīdānīṃ punarbhavaḥ | 2

Wal 4.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate || āgamayānanda yena pāṭaligrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 4.2 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt || atha bhagavān magadheṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caran pāṭaligrāmakam anuprāptaḥ pāṭaligrāmake viharati pāṭalake caitye ||

Wal 4.3 aśrauṣuḥ pāṭaligrāmīyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo bhagavān gautamo magadheṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caran pāṭaligrāmakam anuprāptaḥ pāṭaligrāmake viharati pāṭalake caitye ||

Wal 4.4 śrutvā ca punaḥ saṃghāt saṃghaṃ pūgāt pūgaṃ saṃgamya samāgamya pāṭaligrāmakān niṣkramya yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagmur upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdan ||

Wal 4.5 ekāntaniṣaṇṇān pāṭaligrāmīyakān brāhmaṇagṛhapatīn bhagavān idam avocat ||

Wal 4.6 pañceme brāhmaṇagṛhapataya ādīnavāḥ pramāde || katame pañca ||

Wal 4.7 iha brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor mahatīṃ bhogajyāniṃ nigacchati || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor mahatīṃ bhogajyāniṃ nigacchati || ayaṃ prathama ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.8 punar aparaṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor yāṃ yām eva pariṣadam upasaṃkrāmati yadi vā kṣatriyapariṣadaṃ yadi vā brāhmaṇapariṣadaṃ yadi vā gṛhapatipariṣadaṃ yadi vā śramaṇapariṣadaṃ tatra tatra madgur upasaṃkrāmaty anudagro ’viśāradaḥ || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor yāṃ yām eva pariṣadam upasaṃkrāmati pūrvavad yāvad aviśāradaḥ || ayaṃ dvitīya ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.9 punar aparaṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattasya pramādādhikaraṇahetor digvidikṣu pāpako ’varṇo ’kīrtiśabdaśloko ’bhyudgacchati || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattasya pramādādhikaraṇahetor digvidikṣu pāpako ’varṇo ’kīrtiśabdaśloko ’bhyudgacchati || ayaṃ tṛtīya ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.10 punar aparaṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor vipratisārī kālaṃ karoti || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetor vipratisārī kālaṃ karoti || ayaṃ caturtha ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.11 punar aparaṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetoḥ kāyasya bhedān narakeṣūpapadyate || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ pramattaḥ pramādādhikaraṇahetoḥ kāyasya bhedān narakeṣūpapadyate || ayaṃ pañcama ādīnavaḥ pramāde ||

Wal 4.12 pañca tv ime brāhmaṇagṛhapataya ānuśaṃsā apramāde || katame pañca ||

Wal 4.13 iha brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor na mahatīṃ bhogajyāniṃ nigacchati || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor na mahatīṃ bhogajyāniṃ nigacchati || ayaṃ prathama ānuśaṃso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.14 punar aparaṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor yāṃ yām eva pariṣadam upasaṃkrāmati yadi vā kṣatriyapariṣadaṃ yadi vā brāhmaṇapariṣadaṃ yadi vā gṛhapatipariṣadaṃ yadi vā śramaṇapariṣadaṃ tatra tatrāmadgur upasaṃkrāmaty udagro viśāradaḥ || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor yāṃ yām eva pariṣadam upasaṃkrāmati pūrvavad yāvad viśāradaḥ || ayaṃ dvitīya ānuśaṃso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.15 punar aparaṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramattasyāpramādādhikaraṇahetor digvidikṣūdāraḥ kalyāṇaḥ kīrtiśabdaśloko ’bhyudgacchati || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramattasyāpramādādhikaraṇahetor digvidikṣūdāraḥ kalyāṇaḥ kīrtiśabdaśloko ’bhyudgacchati || ayaṃ tṛtīya ānuśaṃso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.16 punar aparaṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor na vipratisārī kālaṃ karoti || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetor na vipratisārī kālaṃ karoti || ayaṃ caturtha ānuśaṃso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.17 punar aparaṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetoḥ kāyasya bhedāt sugatau svargaloke deveṣūpapadyate || yad brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo ’pramatto ’pramādādhikaraṇahetoḥ kāyasya bhedāt sugatau svargaloke deveṣūpapadyate || ayaṃ pañcama ānuśaṃso ’pramāde ||

Wal 4.18 atha bhagavān pāṭaligrāmīyakān brāhmaṇagṛhapatīn dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati || anekaparyāyeṇa dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṃpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt ||

Wal 4.19 atha pāṭaligrāmīyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapataya utthāyāsanād ekāṃsam uttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃs tenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocan || adhivāsayatv asmākaṃ bhagavān āvasathe rātriṃvāsāya || adhivāsayati bhagavān pāṭaligrāmīyakānāṃ brāhmaṇagṛhapatīnāṃ tūṣṇīṃbhāvena ||

Wal 4.20 atha pāṭaligrāmīyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayo bhagavatas tūṣṇīṃbhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntāḥ ||

Wal 5.1 atha bhagavān aciraprakrāntān pāṭaligrāmīyakān brāhmaṇagṛhapatīn viditvā bahir āvasathasya pādau prakṣālyāvasathaṃ praviśya nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 5.2 tena samayena varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātra udyuktaḥ pāṭaligrāmakaṃ nagaraṃ māpayituṃ vṛjīnāṃ pratighātārtham || tadā pāṭaligrāmake mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastuni pratigṛhṇanti ||

Wal 5.3 paryaṅkam ābhujyarjuṃ kāyaṃ praṇidhāya pratimukhaṃ smṛtim upasthāpyādrākṣīd bhagavān āvasathe divāvihāropagato divyena cakṣuṣā viśuddhenātikrāntamānuṣeṇa pāṭaligrāmake mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti || dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ sāyāhne pratisaṃlayanād vyutthāyāvasathād avatīryāvasathapracchāyāyāṃ purastād bhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 5.4 niṣadya bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

ka ānandodyuktaḥ pāṭaligrāmakaṃ nagaraṃ māpayitum ||

Wal 5.5 varṣākāro bhadanta brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātra udyuktaḥ pāṭaligrāmakaṃ nagaraṃ māpayituṃ vṛjīnāṃ pratighātārtham ||

Wal 5.6 sādhu sādhv ānanda + + varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro yathā devais trāyastriṃśaiḥ sārdham + + + + + + + ||

Wal 5.7 atrāham ānandādrākṣam āvasathe divāvihāropagataḥ pāṭaligrāmake mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti ||

Wal 5.8 yasminn ānanda pradeśe mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti mahāśakyānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tasmin pradeśe cittaṃ krāmati yaduta vāsāya ||

Wal 5.9 yasmin pradeśe madhyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti madhyānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tasmin pradeśe cittaṃ krāmati yaduta vāsāya ||

Wal 5.10 yasmin pradeśe nīcā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti nīcānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tasmin pradeśe cittaṃ krāmati yaduta vāsāya ||

Wal 5.11 asminn ānanda pāṭaligrāmake mahāśakyamahāśakyā devatā vastūni pratigṛhṇanti || asmin pradeśe mahāśakyānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ cittaṃ kramiṣyati yaduta vāsāya ||

Wal 5.12 yāvad evānandāryā āvāsā āryā vyavahārā āryā vāṇir yathaitad agraṃ bhaviṣyati puṭabhedanānāṃ yaduta pāṭaliputraṃ nagaraṃ ||

Wal 5.13 tasya trayo ’ntarāyā veditavyā agnito ’py udakato ’py abhyantarato ’pi mithobhedāt ||

Wal 6.1 aśrauṣīd varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātraḥ || bhagavān gautamo magadheṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caran pāṭaligrāmakam anuprāptaḥ pāṭaligrāmake viharati pāṭalake caitye || paryupāsate taṃ pāṭaligrāmīyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayaḥ ||

Wal 6.2 śrutvā ca punaḥ pāṭaligrāmakān niṣkramya yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavatā sārdhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ saṃmodanīṃ saṃraṃjanīṃ vividhāṃ kathāṃ vyatisāryaikānte nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 6.3 ekāntaniṣaṇṇaṃ varṣākāraṃ brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātraṃ bhagavān dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati || anekaparyāyeṇa dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṃpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt ||

Wal 6.4 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātra utthāyāsanād ekāṃsam uttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃs tenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 6.5 adhivāsayatu me bhavāṅ gautamaḥ śvo bhaktena sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena || adhivāsayati bhagavān varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasya tūṣṇīṃbhāvena ||

Wal 6.6 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro bhagavatas tūṣṇīṃbhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 6.7 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātras tām eva rātriṃ śuciṃ praṇītaṃ khādanīyabhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyam evotthāyāsanakāni prajñapyodakamaṇiṃ pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālam ārocayati || samayo bho gautamo sadyo bhaktaṃ yasyedānīṃ bhavāṅ gautamaḥ kālaṃ manyate ||

Wal 6.8 atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya bhikṣusaṃghaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasya bhaktābhisāras tenopajagāma || upetya purastād bhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 6.9 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātraḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ santarpayati saṃpravārayati || śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ santarpayitvā saṃpravārayitvā bhagavantaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastam apanītapātraṃ sauvarṇaṃ bhṛṅgāraṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purato ’sthāt || āyācamāna evaṃ cāha ||

Wal 6.10 ito dānād yaḥ puṇyābhiṣyandaḥ kuśalābhiṣyandaḥ sa bhavatu pāṭaliputravāstavyānāṃ devatānāṃ dīrgharātram arthāya hitāya sukhāya || teṣāñ ca nāmnā dakṣiṇām ādiśasva ||

Wal 6.11 atha bhagavān varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasya tad dānam anayābhyanumodanayābhyanumodate ||

Wal 6.12 yo devatāḥ pūjayati
śrāddhaḥ puruṣapudgalaḥ ||
śāstur vākyakaro bhavati
buddhair etat praśaṃsitam |

Wal 6.13 yasmin pradeśe medhāvī
vāsaṃ kalpayati paṇḍitaḥ ||
śīlavantaṃ bhojayitvā
dakṣiṇām ādiśet tataḥ |

Wal 6.14 te mānitā mānayanti
pūjitāḥ pūjayanti ca ||
athainam anukampanti
mātā putram ivaurasam ||
devānukampitappoṣaḥ
sukhī bhadrāṇi paśyati |

Wal 7.1 atha bhagavān varṣākāraṃ brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātraṃ dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṃpraharṣayitvotthāyāsanāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 7.2 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro yat tatrotsīdanadharmaṃ tat sarvaṃ visarjanadharmam iti kṛtvā bhagavantaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddhaḥ ||

Wal 7.3 atha varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasyaitad abhavat ||

yena dvāreṇa śramaṇo gautamaḥ prathamato niṣkramiṣyati tam ahaṃ gautamadvāraṃ māpayiṣyāmi yena tīrthena śramaṇo gautamaḥ prathamato nadīṃ gaṅgām uttariṣyati tam ahaṃ gautamatīrthaṃ māpayiṣyāmi ||

Wal 7.4 atha bhagavān varṣākārasya brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātrasya cetasā cittam ājñāya paścimena dvāreṇa niṣkramyottareṇānvāvṛtto yena nadī gaṅgā ||

Wal 7.5 tena khalu samayena māgadhakā manuṣyā nadīṃ gaṅgām uttaranty api pratyuttaranty apy ekatyāḥ śalmaliphaleṣv ekatyā alābuniḥśrayaṇikābhir ekatyās tḥlabimbopanair ekatyāś chāgalakair dṛtibhiḥ ||

Wal 7.6 atha bhagavata etad abhavat || kiṃ nu nadīṃ gaṅgām asajyamānaḥ srotaso gacchāmy āho svid apārime tīre ’ntarhitaḥ pārime tīre pratitiṣṭhāmi || atha bhagavāṃs tadrūpaṃ samādhiṃ samāpanno yathā samāhite citte ’pārime tīre ’ntarhitaḥ pārime tīre pratyasthāt ||

Wal 7.7 atha varṣākāro brāhmaṇamagadhamahāmātro yena dvāreṇa bhagavān niṣkrāntas tad gautamadvāraṃ māpayati yena tīrthena bhagavān nadīṃ gaṅgām uttīrṇas tad gautamatīrthaṃ māpayati ||

Wal 7.8 athānyataro bhikṣus tasyāṃ velāyāṃ gāthāṃ babhāṣe |

Wal 7.9 ye taranti hy ārṇavaṃ saraḥ
setuṃ kṛtvā visṛjya palvalāni ||
kolaṃ hi janāḥ prabadhnate
tīrṇā medhāvino janāḥ |

Wal 7.10 uttīrṇo bhagavān buddho
brāhmaṇas tiṣṭhati sthale ||
bhikṣavaḥ parisnāyanti
kolaṃ badhnanti śrāvakāḥ |

Wal 7.11 kiṃ kuryād udapānena
āpaś cet sarvato yadi ||
chittveha mūlaṃ tṛṣṇāyāḥ
kasya paryeṣaṇāṃ caret |

Wal 8.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 8.2 āgamyānanda yena kuṭigrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 8.3 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 8.4 atha bhagavān yena kuṭigrāmakas tena caryāṃ prakrāntaḥ || anupūrveṇa caryāñ caraṅ kuṭigrāmakam anuprāptaḥ kuṭigrāmake viharaty uttareṇa grāmasya śiṃśapāvane ||

Wal 8.5 tatra bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 8.6 itīmāni bhikṣavaḥ śīlāny ayaṃ samādhir iyaṃ prajñā || śīlaparibhāvitaḥ samādhiś cirasthitiko bhavati || prajñāparibhāvitaṃ cittaṃ samyag eva vimucyate rāgadveṣamohebhyaḥ ||

Wal 8.7 evaṃ samyaksuvimuktacitta āryaśrāvakaḥ samyag eva prajānāti || kṣīṇā me jātir uṣitaṃ brahmacaryaṃ kṛtaṃ karaṇīyaṃ nāparam asmād bhavaṃ prajānāmi ||

Wal 9.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 9.2 āgamayānanda yena nādikā ||

Wal 9.3 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 9.4 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāñ caran nādikām anuprāpto nādikāyāṃ viharati kuñjikāvasathe ||

Wal 9.5 tena samayena nādikāyā mahato janakāyasya māry utthitābhūt || tathā hi karkaṭaka upāsakaḥ kālagataḥ ||

Wal 9.6 nikaṭa upāsakaḥ kaḍaṅgaraḥ kātyarṣabhaś cārur upacārur ariṣṭa upāriṣṭo bhadraḥ subhadro yaśo yaśodatto yaśottaro ’pi kālagataḥ ||

Wal 9.7 atha saṃbahulā bhikṣavaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya nādikāṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣan ||

Wal 9.8 aśrauṣuḥ saṃbahulā bhikṣavo nādikāṃ piṇḍāya carantaḥ || asyāṃ nādikāyāṃ mahāñ janakāyo mṛtaḥ || tathā hi karkaṭaka upāsakaḥ kālagato nikaṭo kaḍaṅgaraḥ kātyarṣabhaś cārur upacārur ariṣṭa upāriṣṭo bhadraḥ subhadro yaśo yaśodatto yaśottaraḥ kālagataḥ ||

Wal 9.9 śrutvā ca punar nādikāṃ piṇḍāya caritvā kṛtabhaktakṛtyāḥ paścādbhaktapiṇḍapātāḥ pratikrāntāḥ || pātracīvaraṃ pratiśāmya pādau prakṣālya yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagmuḥ || upetya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdan ||

Wal 9.10 ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ saṃbahulā bhikṣavo bhagavantam idam avocan ||

Wal 9.11 iha vayaṃ bhadanta saṃbahulā bhikṣavaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya nādikāṃ piṇḍāya prāviśāma || aśrauṣma vayam asyāṃ nādikāyāṃ karkaṭaka upāsakaḥ kālagataḥ pūrvavad yāvad yaśodatto yaśottaraḥ kālagataḥ teṣāṃ bhadanta kā gatiḥ kopapattiḥ ko ’bhisaṃparāyaḥ ||

Wal 9.12 karkaṭaka upāsakaḥ pañcānām avarabhāgīyānāṃ saṃyojanānāṃ prahāṇād aupapādukās tatra parinirvāyy anāgāmy anāvṛttidharmā punar imaṃ lokaṃ ||

Wal 9.13 nikaṭaḥ kaḍaṅgaraḥ pūrvavad yāvad yaśottara upāsakaḥ pañcānām avarabhāgīyānāṃ pūrvavad yāvat punar imaṃ lokam ||

Wal 9.14 santi bhikṣavo nādikāyām ardhatṛtīyāny upāsakaśatāni kālagatāni yāni pañcānām avarabhāgīyānāṃ saṃyojanānāṃ prahāṇād aupapādukās tatra parinirvāyiṇo ’nāgāmino ’nāvṛttidharmāṇaḥ punar imaṃ lokam ||

Wal 9.15 sātirekāṇi bhikṣavo nādikāyāṃ tryupāsakaśatāni abhyatītāni kālagatāni yāni trayāṇāṃ saṃyojanānāṃ prahāṇād rāgadveṣamohānāṃ ca tanutvāt kālaṃ kṛtvā sakṛdāgāminaḥ sakṛd imaṃ lokam āgamya duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyanti ||

Wal 9.16 sātirekāṇy asyāṃ nādikāyāṃ pañcopāsakaśatāny abhyatītāni kālagatāni yāni trayāṇāṃ saṃyojanānāṃ prahāṇāc chrotaāpannā avinipātadharmāṇo niyataṃ saṃbodhiparāyaṇāḥ saptakṛtvaḥparamāḥ saptakṛtvo devāṃś ca manuṣyāṃś ca saṃdhāvya saṃsṛtya duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyanti ||

Wal 9.17 kālagatāḥ kālagatā iti yūyaṃ bhikṣavas tathāgataṃ prakṣyatha viheṭhayiṣyatha tathāgataṃ na punar anena tathāgat. + + + + + + + + jātasyāvaśyaṃ kālakriyā ||

Wal 9.18 kim atrāścaryam || utpādād vā tathāgatānām anutpādād vā sthitaiveyaṃ dharmatā dharmasthitaye dhātūṃs tāṃs tathāgataḥ svayam abhijñāyābhisaṃbuddhyākhyāti prajñāpayati prasthāpayati vibhajati vivaraty uttānīkaroti deśayati saṃprakāśayati ||

Wal 9.19 yadutāsmin satīdaṃ bhavaty asyotpādād idam utpadyate yadutāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā yāvat samudayo nirodhaś ca bhavati ||

Wal 9.20

Wal 9.21 api dharmādarśaṃ nāma dharmaparyāyaṃ deśayiṣye || taṃ śṛṇuta sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasi kuruta bhāṣiṣye || dharmādarśo dharmaparyāyaḥ katamaḥ || buddhe dharme saṃghe ’vetyaprasādena samanvāgato bhavaty āryakāntaiḥ śīlaiḥ samanvāgato bhavati || ayam ucyate dharmādarśo dharmaparyāyaḥ || dharmādarśo dharmaparyāya iti me yad uktaṃ yuṣmākaṃ bhikṣavas tad uktam ||

Wal 9.22

Wal 10.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate || āgamayānanda yena vaiśālī ||

Wal 10.2 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 10.3 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caran vaiśālim anuprāpto vaiśālyāṃ viharaty āmrapālivane ||

Wal 10.4 aśrauṣīd āmrapālir gaṇikā || bhagavāṅ gautamo vaiśālīm anuprāpto vaiśālyāṃ viharaty asmākam evāmravane ||

Wal 10.5 śrutvā ca punaḥ sarvālaṃkārair alaṃkṛtā strīgaṇam anvāhiṇḍayitvā bhadraṃ yānam adhiruhya vaiśālyā niryāti bhagavato ’ntikenopadarśanāya bhagavantaṃ paryupāsanāyai ||

Wal 10.6 tasyā yāvad yānabhūmis tāvad yānena gatvā yānād avatīrya padbhyām eva yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkrāntā ||

Wal 10.7 adrākṣīd bhagavān anekaśatabhikṣuparivāre sanniṣaṇṇa āmrapāliṃ dūrād āgacchantīṃ dṛṣṭvā ca punar bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 10.8 ātāpino bhikṣavo viharata saṃprajānāḥ pratismṛtāḥ || āmrapālir gaṇikātrāgatā ||

Wal 10.9 kathaṃ ca bhikṣur ātāpī bhavati ||

Wal 10.10 iha bhikṣur utpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ prahāṇāya cchandaṃ janayati vyāyacchate vīryam ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti pradadhāti ||

anutpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām anutpādāya cchandaṃ janayati pūrvavat ||

anutpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām utpādāya cchandaṃ janayati pūrvavat ||

utpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ sthitaye bhūyobhāvatāyā asaṃpramoṣāya paripūraṇāya vaipulyāya cchandaṃ janayati pūrvavat || ayaṃ bhikṣur ātāpī bhavati ||

Wal 10.11 kathañ ca bhikṣuḥ saṃprajāno bhavati ||

Wal 10.12 iha bhikṣur abhikrānte pratikrānte saṃprajāno bhavaty ālokite vilokite saṃmiñjite prasārite saṃghāṭīcīvarapātradhāraṇe gate sthite niṣaṇṇe śayite jāgarite bhāṣite tūṣṇīṃbhāve supte śrame viśrame saṃprajāno bhavati || ayaṃ bhikṣur saṃprajāno bhavati ||

Wal 10.13 kathañ ca bhikṣuḥ pratismṛto bhavati ||

Wal 10.14 iha bhikṣur adhyātmaṃ kāye kāyānupaśyī viharaty ātāpī saṃprajānaḥ smṛtimān vinīyābhidhyā loke daurmanasyam || bahirdhā kāye ’dhyātmabahirdhā kāye ’dhyātmaṃ vedanāsu bahirdhā vedanāsv adhyātmabahirdhā vedanāsv adhyātmaṃ citte bahirdhā citte ’dhyātmabahirdhā citte ’dhyātmaṃ dharmeṣu bahirdhā dharmeṣv adhyātmabahirdhā dharmeṣu dharmānupaśyī viharaty ātāpī saṃprajānaḥ smṛtimān vinīyābhidhyā loke daurmanasyam || ayaṃ bhikṣuḥ pratismṛto bhavati ||

Wal 10.15 ātāpino bhikṣavo viharata saṃprajānāḥ pratismṛtāḥ || āmrapālir gaṇikātrāgatety eva mayākhyātam ||

Wal 10.16 athāmrapālir yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 10.17 ekāntaniṣaṇṇām āmrapāliṃ bhagavān dhārmyā kathayā pūrvavad yāvat saṃpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt ||

Wal 10.18 atha āmrapālir utthāyāsanād yena bhagavāṃs tenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 10.19 adhivāsayatu me bhagavāñ śvo bhaktena sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena ||

Wal 10.20 adhivāsayati bhagavāṃ tūṣṇīṃbhāvena || atha āmrapālir bhagavatas tūṣṇīṃbhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntā ||

Wal 11.1 aśrauṣur vaiśālakā licchavayaḥ || bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caran vaiśālīm anuprāpto vaiśālyāṃ viharaty āmrapālivane ||

Wal 11.2 śrutvā pratyekapratyekaṃ bhadreṣu yāneṣv adhiruhya … māṇābhir

Wal 11.3 ekatyā nīlāśvā nīlarathā nīlapragrahapratodā nīloṣṇīṣā nīlacchatrakhaḍgakośā nīlamaṇidaṇḍakacāmarā nīlavastrālaṃkāravilepanā nīlaparivārā

Wal 11.4 ekatyāḥ pītāśvāḥ pītarathāḥ pītapragrahapratodāḥ pītoṣṇīṣāḥ pītacchatrakhaḍgakośāḥ pītamaṇidaṇḍakacāmarāḥ pītavastrālaṃkāravilepanāḥ pītaparivārā ||

Wal 11.5 ekatyā lohitāśvā lohitarathā lohitapragrahapratodā lohitoṣṇīṣā lohitacchatrakhaḍgakośā lohitamaṇidaṇḍakacāmarā lohitavastrālaṃkāravilepanā lohitaparivārā

Wal 11.6 ekatyāḥ śvetāśvāḥ śvetarathāḥ śvetapragrahapratodāḥ śvetoṣṇīṣāḥ śvetacchatrakhaḍgakośāḥ śvetamaṇidaṇḍakacāmarāḥ śvetavastrālaṃkāravilepanāḥ śvetaparivārā

Wal 11.7 uccaśabdaṃ prakṣveḍayanto mahāśabdaṃ prakṣveḍayanto vaiśālyā niṣkramya yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagmur bhagavaddarśanāya bhagavantaṃ paryupāsanāyai ||

Wal 11.8 adrākṣīd bhagavān vaiśalakāl licchavīn dūrād evāgacchato dṛṣṭvā ca punar bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 11.9 … vaiśālakāl licchavīn paśyatha || anayarddhyā …

Wal 11.10 teṣāṃ yāvad yānabhūmis tāvad yānena gatvā yānād avatīrya padbhyām eva yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagmur upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdan ||

Wal 11.11 ekāntaniṣaṇṇān vaiśālakāl licchavīn bhagavān dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati ||

Wal 11.12 tena khalu samayena paiṅgiko māṇavas tasmin samāje sanniṣaṇṇo ’bhūt sannipatitaḥ || atha paiṅgiko māṇava utthāyāsanād ekāṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃs tenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 11.13 pratibhāti me bhagavan pratibhāti me sugata ||

Wal 11.14 pratibhātu te paiṅgiketi bhagavān avocat ||

Wal 11.21 atha bhagavān vaiśālakāl licchavīn dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṃpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt ||

Wal 11.22 atha vaiśālakā licchavaya utthāyāsanād ekāṃsam uttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃs tenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocan ||

Wal 11.23 adhivāsayatu no bhagavāñ śvo bhaktena sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena ||

Wal 11.24 nimantrito ’smi vāsiṣṭhās tatprathamata āmrapālyā ||

Wal 11.25 bhadantāmrapālyāmbakayā a … punar vayaṃ bhadantopasthāsyāmo bhagavantaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ ca ||

Wal 11.26 kalyāṇam idaṃ vāsiṣṭhā uktam ||

Wal 11.27 atha vaiśālakā licchavayo bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntāḥ ||

Wal 12.1 athāmrapālis tām eva rātriṃ śuciṃ praṇītaṃ khādanīyabhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyam evotthāya āsanakāni prajñapyodakamaṇiṃ pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālam ārocayati ||

Wal 12.2 samayo bho gautamo sadyo bhaktaṃ yasyedānīṃ bhavāṅ gautamaḥ kālaṃ manyate ||

Wal 12.3 atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya bhikṣusaṃghaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yenāmrapālyā gaṇikāyā bhaktābhisāras tenopajagāma || upetya purastād bhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 12.4 athāmrapāliḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ santarpayati saṃpravārayati || śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ santarpayitvā saṃpravārayitvā

Wal 12.5 bhagavantaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastam apanītapātraṃ nīcatarakam āsanaṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purato niṣaṇṇā dharmaśravaṇāya ||

Wal 12.6 atha bhagavān āmrapālyās tad dānam anayābhyanumodanayābhyanumodate |

Wal 12.7 dadat priyo bhavati bhajanti taṃ janāḥ
kīrtiṃ samāpnoti yaśaś ca vardhate ||
amadgubhūtaḥ pariṣadaṃ vigāhate
viśārado bhavati naro hy amatsarī |

Wal 12.8 tasmād dhi dānāni dadati paṇḍitā
vinīya mātsaryamalaṃ sukhaiṣiṇaḥ ||
te dīrgharātraṃ tridaśe pratiṣṭhitā
devānāṃ svabhāvagatā ramanti te |

Wal 12.9 kṛtāyuṣāḥ kṛtakuśalā itaś cyutāḥ
svayaṃprabhā anuvicaranti nandane ||
te tatra krīḍanti ramanti cobhayaṃ
samarpitāḥ kāmaguṇais tu pañcabhiḥ ||
śrutveha vākyam asitasya tāyinaḥ
svarge ramante sugatasya śrāvakāḥ |

Wal 12.10 atha bhagavān āmrapāliṃ dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṃpraharṣayitvotthāyāsanāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 13.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 13.2 āgamayānanda yena veṇugrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 13.3 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 13.4 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caran veṇugrāmakam anuprāpto veṇugrāmake viharaty uttareṇa grāmasya śiṃśapāvane ||

Wal 13.5 tena khalu samayena durbhikṣam abhūt kṛcchraḥ kāntāro durlabhaḥ piṇḍako yācanakena ||

Wal 13.6 tatra bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 13.7 etarhi bhikṣavo durbhikṣaṃ kṛcchraḥ kāntāro durlabho piṇḍako yācanakena ||

Wal 13.8 eta yūyaṃ bhikṣavo yathāsaṃstutikayā yathāsaṃlaptikayā yathāsaṃpremikayā vaiśālīsamantakena vṛjigrāmakeṣu varṣām upagacchata ||

Wal 13.9 aham apy asminn eva veṇugrāmake varṣām upagamiṣyāmy ānandena bhikṣuṇopasthāyakena || mā sarva eva piṇḍakena klāmatha ||

Wal 13.10 evaṃ bhadanteti te bhikṣavo bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya

Wal 13.11 yathāsaṃstutikayā yathāsaṃlaptikayā yathāsaṃpremikayā vaiśālīsamantakena vṛjigrāmakeṣu varṣām upagatāḥ ||

Wal 14.1 bhagavān tatraiva veṇugrāmake varṣām upagata ānandena bhikṣuṇopasthāyakena ||

Wal 14.2 tasya khalu varṣopagatasyotpannaḥ khara ābādhaḥ pragāḍhā vedanā māraṇāntikā ||

Wal 14.3 atha bhagavata etad abhavat ||

Wal 14.4 utpanno me khara ābādhaḥ pragāḍhā vedanā māraṇāntikā viprakrāntaś ca bhikṣusaṃghaḥ ||

Wal 14.5 na mama pratirūpaṃ syād yad ahaṃ viprakrānte bhikṣusaṃghe parinirvāyām || yan nv ahaṃ tata ekatyā vedanā vīryeṇa pratiprasrabhya sarvanimittānām amanasikārād ānimittaṃ cetaḥsamādhiṃ kāyena sākṣīkṛtvopasaṃpadya vihareyam ||

Wal 14.6 atha bhagavān tata ekatyā vedanā vīryeṇa pratiprasrabhya sarvanimittānām amanasikārād animittaṃ cetaḥsamādhiṃ kāyena sākṣīkṛtvopasaṃpadya vyahārṣīt || tena tathāgatasya kṣemaṇīyatarañ cābhūd yāpanīyatarañ ca ||

Wal 14.7 athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ sāyāhne pratisaṃlayanād vyutthāya yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt ||

Wal 14.8 ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 14.9 api me bhadanta m. … lapante bhagavata imam evaṃ .r … āśvāsamātram || na tāvad bhagavān parinirvāsyati yāvad bhagavān bhikṣusaṃgh. …

Wal 14.10 yasyānandaivaṃ syāt || mamāsti bhikṣusaṃghaḥ || ahaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ parihariṣyāmīti …

Wal 14.11 mama khalv ānanda naivaṃ bhavati || mamāsti bhikṣusaṃghaḥ || ahaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ parihariṣyāmīti …

Wal 14.12 …

Wal 14.13 tadyathā catvāri smṛtyupasthānāni catvāri samyakprahāṇāni catvāra ṛddhipādāḥ pañcendriyāṇi pañca balāni sapta bodhyaṅgāny āryāṣṭāṅgo mārgaḥ ||

Wal 14.14 na tatrānanda tathāgatasya dharmeṣv ācāryamuṣṭir yaṃ tathāgataḥ praticchādayitavyaṃ manyeta || kaccin me pare na vidyur iti ||

Wal 14.15 utpannaḥ kadāpi tathāgatasya khara ābādhaḥ pragāḍhā vedanā māraṇāntikā ||

Wal 14.16 tasya ma etad abhavat || utpanno me khara ābādhaḥ pragāḍhā vedanā māraṇāntikā viprakrāntaś ca bhikṣusaṃghaḥ ||

Wal 14.17 na mama pratirūpaṃ syād yad ahaṃ viprakrānte bhikṣusaṃghe parinirvāyām || yan nv ahaṃ tata ekatyā vedanā vīryeṇa pratiprasrabhya sarvanimittānām amanasikārād animittaṃ cetaḥsamādhiṃ kāyena sākṣīkṛtvopasaṃpadya vihareyam ||

Wal 14.18 so ’haṃ tata ekatyā vedanā vīryeṇa pratiprasrabhya sarvanimittānām amanasikārād animittaṃ cetaḥsamādhiṃ kāyena sākṣīkṛtvopasaṃpadya vyahārṣam || tena tathāgatasya kṣemaṇīyatarañ cābhūd yāpanīyatarañ ca ||

Wal 14.19 punar aparam ānanda tathāgato vṛddho jīrṇatāṃ prāpto ’śītike vayasi vartate dvaidhāniśrayeṇa yāpyate || tadyathā jīrṇaṃ śakaṭaṃ dvaidhāniśrayeṇa yāpyata evam eva tathāgato vṛddho jīrnatāṃ prāpto ’śītike vayasi vartate dvaidhāniśrayeṇa yāpyate ||

Wal 14.20 mā tasmāt tvam ānanda śoca mā klāma || kasmād eva tat || kuta etal labhyaṃ yat taj jātaṃ bhūtaṃ kṛtaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ vedayitaṃ pratītyasamutpannaṃ kṣayadharmaṃ vyayadharmaṃ virodhadharmaṃ pralokadharmaṃ na prarujyate || nedaṃ sthānaṃ vidyate ||

Wal 14.21 prāg eva bhikṣavo mayākhyātaṃ sarvair iṣṭaiḥ kāntaiḥ priyair manāpair nānābhāvo bhaviṣyati vinābhāvo viprayogo visaṃyogaḥ ||

Wal 14.22 tasmād ānandaitarhi mama vātyayād ātmadvīpair vihartavyam ātmaśaraṇair dharmadvīpair dharmaśaraṇair ananyadvīpair ananyaśaraṇaiḥ || tat kasmād dhetoḥ ||

Wal 14.23 ye kecid ānandaitarhi mama vātyayād ātmadvīpā ātmaśaraṇā dharmadvīpā dharmaśaraṇā ananyadvīpā ananyaśaraṇās te ’graṃ bhaviṣyanti yaduta mama śrāvakāṇāṃ śikṣākāmānāṃ ||

Wal 14.24 kathaṃ cānanda bhikṣur ātmadvīpo bhavaty ātmaśaraṇo dharmadvīpo dharmaśaraṇo ’nanyadvīpo ’nanyaśaraṇaḥ ||

Wal 14.25 iha bhikṣur adhyātmaṃ kāye kāyānupaśyī viharaty ātāpī saṃprajānaḥ smṛtimān vinīyābhidhyā loke daurmanasyam || bahirdhā kāye ’dhyātmabahirdhā kāye ’dhyātmaṃ vedanāsu bahirdhā vedanāsv adhyātmabahirdhā vedanāsv adhyātmaṃ citte bahirdhā citte ’dhyātmabahirdhā citte ’dhyātmaṃ dharmeṣu bahirdhā dharmeṣv adhyātmabahirdhā dharmeṣu dharmānupaśyī viharaty ātāpī saṃprajānaḥ smṛtimān vinīyābhidhyā loke daurmanasyam ||

Wal 14.26 evaṃ hi bhikṣur ātmadvīpo bhavaty ātmaśaraṇo dharmadvīpo dharmaśaraṇo ’nanyadvīpo ’nanyaśaraṇaḥ ||

Hier im Tib. Uddāna

Wal 15.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 15.2 āgamayānanda yena vaiśālī ||

Wal 15.3 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 15.4 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caran vaiśālīm anuprāpto vaiśālyāṃ viharati markaṭahradatīre kūṭāgāraśālāyām ||

Wal 15.5 atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya vaiśālīṃ piṇḍāya prāviśad āyuṣmatānandena paścācchramaṇena ||

Wal 15.6 atha bhagavān vaiśālīṃ piṇḍāya caritvā kṛtabhaktakṛtyaḥ paścādbhaktapiṇḍapātaḥpratikrāntaḥ ||

Wal 15.7 pātracīvaraṃ pratiśamayya yena cāpālaṃ caityaṃ tenopajagāma || upetyānyataraṃ vṛkṣamūlaṃ niśritya niṣaṇṇo divāvihārāya ||

Wal 15.8 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 15.9 ramaṇīyānanda vaiśālī vṛjibhūmiś cāpālaṃ caityaṃ saptāmrakaṃ bahupattrakaṃ gautamanyagrodhaḥ śālavanaṃ dhurānikṣepaṇaṃ mallānāṃ makuṭabandhanaṃ caityam || citro jaṃbudvīpo madhuraṃ jīvitaṃ manuṣyāṇām ||

Wal 15.10 yasya kasyacic catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtā ākāṃkṣamāṇaḥ sa kalpaṃ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṃ vā || tathāgatasyānanda catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtāḥ || ākāṃkṣamāṇas tathāgataḥ kalpaṃ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṃ vā ||

Wal 15.11 evam ukta āyuṣmān ānandas tūṣṇīm abhūt || dvir api trir api bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 15.12 ramaṇīyānanda vaiśālī vṛjibhūmiś cāpālaṃ caityaṃ saptāmrakaṃ bahupattrakaṃ gautamanyagrodhaḥ śālavanaṃ dhurānikṣepaṇaṃ mallānāṃ makuṭabandhanaṃ caityam || citro jaṃbudvīpo madhuraṃ jīvitaṃ manuṣyāṇām ||

Wal 15.13 yasya kasyacic catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtā ākāṃkṣamāṇaḥ sa kalpaṃ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṃ vā || tathāgatasyānanda catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtāḥ || ākāṃkṣamāṇas tathāgataḥ kalpaṃ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṃ vā ||

Wal 15.14 dvir api trir apy āyuṣmān ānandas tūṣṇīm ||

Wal 15.15 atha bhagavata etad abhavat || sphuṭo batāyam ānando bhikṣur māreṇa pāpīyasā yatredānīṃ yāvat trir apy audārike avabhāsanimitte prāviṣkriyamāṇe na śaknoti tannimittam ājñātuṃ yathāpi tataḥ sphuṭo māreṇa pāpīyasā ||

Wal 15.16 iti viditvāyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 15.17 gacchānandānyataravṛkṣamūlaṃ niśritya vihara mā ubhāv apy ākīrṇavihāriṇau bhaviṣyāvaḥ ||

Wal 15.18 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutyānyatamavṛkṣamūlaṃ niśritya niṣaṇṇo divāvihārāya ||

Wal 16.1 sa māraḥ pāpīyān yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ || upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt || ekāntasthito māraḥ pāpīyān bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 16.2 parinirvāhi bhagavan parinirvāṇasamayaḥ sugatasya ||

Wal 16.3

Wal 16.4 kasmāt tvaṃ pāpīyann evaṃ vadasi || parinirvāhi bhagavan parinirvāṇasamayaḥ sugatasya ||

Wal 16.5 eko ’yaṃ bhadanta samayaḥ || bhagavān uruvilvāyāṃ viharati nadyā nairañjanāyās tīre bodhimūle ’cirābhisaṃbuddhaḥ || so ’haṃ yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ ||

Wal 16.6 upetya bhagavantam evaṃ vadāmi || parinirvāhi bhagavan parinirvāṇasamayaḥ sugatasya ||

Wal 16.7 bhagavān evam āha ||

Wal 16.8 na tāvat pāpīyan parinirvāsyāmi yāvan na me śrāvakāḥ paṇḍitā bhaviṣyanti vyaktā medhāvinaḥ || alam utpannotpannānāṃ parapravādināṃ saha dharmeṇa nigrahītāraḥ || alaṃ svasya vādasya paryavadātāro bhikṣavo bhikṣuṇya upāsakā upāsikā vaistārikaṃ ca me brahmacaryaṃ cariṣyanti bahujanyaṃ pṛthubhūtaṃ yāvad devamanuṣyebhyaḥ samyaksaṃprakāśitam ||

Wal 16.9 etarhi bhadanta bhagavataḥ śrāvakāḥ paṇḍitā vyaktā medhāvinaḥ || alam utpannotpannānāṃ parapravādināṃ saha dharmeṇa nigrahītāraḥ svasya vādasya paryavadātāro bhikṣavo bhikṣuṇya upāsakā upāsikā vaistārikaṃ ca te brahmacaryaṃ bāhujanyaṃ pṛthubhūtaṃ yāvad devamanuṣyebhyaḥ samyaksaṃprakāśitam ||

Wal 16.10 tasmād aham evaṃ vadāmi parinirvāhi bhagavan parinirvāṇasamayaḥ sugatasya ||

Wal 16.11 alpotsukas tvaṃ pāpīyan bhava na cirasyedānīṃ tathāgatasya trayāṇāṃ māsānām atyayād anupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati ||

Wal 16.12 atha mārasya pāpīyasa etad abhavat || parinirvāsyate śramaṇo gautama iti viditvā hṛṣṭas tuṣṭa udagraḥ prītisaumanasyajātas tatraivāntarhitaḥ ||

Wal 16.13 atha bhagavata etad abhavat || yan nv ahaṃ tadrūpān ṛddhyabhisaṃskārān abhisaṃskuryāṃ yathā samāhite citte jīvitasaṃskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṃskārān utsṛjeyam ||

Wal 16.14 atha bhagavāṃs tadrūpān ṛddhyabhisaṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti yathā samāhite citte jīvitasaṃskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṃskārān utsṛjati || samanantarotsṛṣṭāyuḥsaṃskāreṣv atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś cābhūd ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 16.15 atha bhagavāṃs tasmāt samādher vyutthāya tasyāṃ velāyāṃ gāthāṃ babhāṣe ||

tulyam atulyaṃ ca saṃbhavaṃ
bhavasaṃskāram apotsṛjan muniḥ ||
adhyātmarataḥ samāhito
hy abhinat kośam ivāṇḍasaṃbhavaḥ |

Wal 17.1 athāyuṣmān ānando yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt || ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 17.2 ko bhadanta hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo yenaitarhy abhūn mahāpṛthivīcāla ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 17.3 aṣṭāv ime hetavo ’ṣṭau pratyayā mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya || katame ’ṣṭau ||

Wal 17.4 iyaṃ mahāpṛthivy apsu pratiṣṭhitā || āpo vāyau pratiṣṭhitā vāyur ākāśe pratiṣṭhitaḥ || bhavaty ānanda samayo yad ākāśe viṣamā vāyavo vānty āpaḥ kṣobhayanti || āpaḥ kṣubdhāḥ pṛthivīṃ cālayanti ||

Wal 17.5 ayaṃ prathamo hetuḥ prathamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.6 punar aparaṃ bhikṣur maharddhiko bhavati mahānubhāvaḥ sa parīttāṃ pṛthivīsaṃjñām adhitiṣṭhaty apramāṇāṃ cāpsaṃjñāṃ sa ākāṃkṣamāṇaḥ pṛthivīṃ cālayati ||

Wal 17.7 bhikṣuṇī devatā vā maharddhikā bhavati mahānubhāvā sā parīttāṃ pṛthivīsaṃjñām adhitiṣṭhaty apramāṇāṃ cāpsaṃjñām ākāṃkṣamāṇā pṛthivīṃ cālayati ||

Wal 17.8 ayaṃ dvitīyo hetur dvitīyaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.9 punar aparaṃ yasmin samaye bodhisatvas tuṣitād devanikāyāc cyutvā mātuḥ kukṣāv avakrāmaty atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavati sarvaś cāyaṃ loka udāreṇāvabhāsena sphuṭo bhavanti ||

Wal 17.10 api tā lokasya lokāntarikā andhatamā andhakāratamisrā yatremau sūryācandramasāv evaṃmaharddhikāv evaṃmahānubhāvāv ābhayābhāṃ na pratyanubhavatas tā api tasmin samaye udāreṇāvabhāsena sphuṭā bhavati ||

Wal 17.11 tatra ye satvā upapannās te tayābhayānyonyaṃ satvaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃjānante || anye ’pi bhavantaḥ satvā ihopapannāḥ || anye ’pi bhavantaḥ satvā ihopapannāḥ ||

Wal 17.12 ayaṃ tṛtīyo hetus tṛtīyaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.13 punar aparaṃ yasmin samaye bodhisatvo mātuḥ kukṣer niṣkrāmaty atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavati pūrvavad yāvad anye ’pi bhavantaḥ satvā ihopapannāḥ ||

Wal 17.14 ayaṃ caturtho hetuś caturthaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.15 punar aparaṃ yasmin samaye bodhisatvo ’nuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim adhigacchaty atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavati pūrvavat ||

Wal 17.16 ayaṃ pañcamo hetuḥ pañcamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.17 punar aparam ānanda yasmin samaye tathāgatas triparivartaṃ dvādaśākāraṃ dhārmyaṃ dharmacakraṃ pravartayaty atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavati pūrvavat ||

Wal 17.18 ayaṃ ṣaṣṭho hetuḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.19 punar aparaṃ yasmin samaye tathāgato jīvitasaṃskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṃskārān utsṛjaty atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālo bhavaty ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 17.20 ayaṃ saptamo hetuḥ saptamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 17.21 punar aparaṃ na cirasyedānīṃ tathāgatasyānupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati || atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavaty ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 17.22 ayam aṣṭamo hetur aṣṭamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 18.1 athāyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 18.2 yathā khalv ahaṃ bhadanta bhagavato bhāṣitasyārtham ājānāmi bhagavataitarhi jīvitasaṃskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṃskārā utsṛṣṭāḥ ||

Wal 18.3 evam etad ānandaivam etad ānanda || etarhy ānanda tathāgatena jīvitasaṃskārān adhiṣṭhāyāyuḥsaṃskārā utsṛṣṭāḥ ||

Wal 18.4 saṃmukhaṃ me bhadanta bhagavato ’ntikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam || yasya kasyacic catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtā ākāṃkṣamāṇaḥ kalpam api tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣam api ||

Wal 18.5 bhagavato bhadanta catvāra ṛddhipādā āsevitā bhāvitā bahulīkṛtā ākāṃkṣamāṇas tathāgatas kalpaṃ vā tiṣṭhet kalpāvaśeṣaṃ vā ||

Wal 18.6 tiṣṭhatu bhagavān kalpaṃ tiṣṭhatu sugataḥ kalpāvaśeṣam ||

Wal 18.7 tavaivānandāparādhas tavaiva duṣkṛtaṃ yas tvaṃ tathāgatasya yāvat trir apy audāre ’vabhāsanimitte prāviṣkriyamāṇe na śaknoṣi taṃ nimittaṃ prativeddhuṃ yathāpi tat sphuṭo māreṇa pāpīyasā ||

Wal 18.8 kiṃ manyasa ānanda bhāṣeta tathāgatas tāṃ vācaṃ yā syād dvaidhavipākyā || no bhadanta ||

Wal 18.9 sādhu sādhv ānanda || asthānam anavakāśo yat tahāgatas tāṃ vācaṃ bhāṣeta yā syād dvaidhavipākyā ||

Wal 19.1 gaccha tvam ānanda yāvanto bhikṣavaś cāpālaṃ caityam upaniśritya viharanti tān sarvān upasthānaśālāyāṃ sannipātaya ||

Wal 19.2 evaṃ bhadanta || āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya yāvanto bhikṣavaś cāpālaṃ caityam upaniśritya viharanti tān sarvān upasthānaśālāyāṃ sannipātya yena bhagavāṃs tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ || upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt ||

Wal 19.3 ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 19.4 yāvanto bhadanta bhikṣavaś cāpālaṃ caityam upaniśritya viharanti sarve ta upasthānaśālāyāṃ niṣaṇṇāḥ sannipatitāḥ || yasyedānīṃ bhagavān kālaṃ manyate ||

Wal 19.5 atha bhagavān yenopasthānaśālā tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ || upasaṃkramya purastād bhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat || niṣadya bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate sma ||

Wal 19.6 anityā bhikṣavaḥ sarvasaṃskārā adhruvā anāśvāsikā vipariṇāmadharmāṇo yāvad alam eva bhikṣavaḥ sarvasaṃskārān saṃskaritum alaṃ virantum ||

Wal 19.7 tasmāt tarhi bhikṣavo ye te dharmā dṛṣṭadharmahitāya saṃvartante dṛṣṭadharmasukhāya saṃparāyahitāya saṃparāyasukhāya te bhikṣubhir udgṛhya paryavāpya tathā tathā dhārayitavyā grāhayitavyā vācayitavyā yathedaṃ brahmacaryaṃ cirasthitikaṃ syāt tad bhaviṣyati bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāyārthāya hitāya sukhāya devamanuṣyāṇāṃ ||

Wal 19.8 katame te dharmā dṛṣṭadharmahitāya saṃvartante dṛṣṭadharmasukhāya saṃparāyahitāya saṃparāyasukhāya te bhikṣubhir udgṛhya pūrvavad yāvad devamanuṣyāṇām ||

Wal 19.9 tadyathā catvāri smṛtyupasthānāni catvāri samyakprahāṇāni catvāra ṛddhipādāḥ pañcendriyāṇi pañca balāni sapta bodhyaṅgāny āryāṣṭāṅgo mārgaḥ ||

Wal 19.10 ime te dharmā dṛṣṭadharmahitāya saṃvartante pūrvavad yāvad devamanuṣyāṇām ||

Wal 20.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 20.2 āgamayānanda yena kuṣṭhagrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 20.3 evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 20.4 bhagavān vaiśālīsāmantakenātikraman dakṣiṇena sarvakāyena nāgāvalokitenāvalokayati ||

Wal 20.5 adrākṣīd āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantaṃ dakṣiṇena sarvakāyena nāgāvalokitena vyavalokayantaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 20.6 nāhetv apratyayaṃ bhadanta tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā nāgāvalokitam avalokayanti || ko bhadanta hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo nāgāvalokitasya ||

Wal 20.7 evam etad ānandaivam etad ānanda || nāhetv apratyayaṃ tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhā dakṣiṇena sarvakāyena nāgāvalokitenāvalokayanti ||

Wal 20.8 idam ānanda tathāgatasya vaiśālyāḥ paścimaṃ darśanaṃ na bhūya iha saṃbuddho vaiśālīm āgamiṣyati || parinirvāṇāya gamiṣyati mallānām upavartanaṃ yamakaśālavanam ||

Wal 20.9 athānyataro bhikṣus tasyāṃ velāyāṃ gāthāṃ babhāṣe ||

Wal 20.10 idam apaścimakaṃ nātha
vaiśālyās tava darśanam ||
na bhūyaḥ sugato buddho
vaiśālīm āgamiṣyati ||
nirvāṇāya prayāto ’yaṃ
mallānām upavartane |

Wal 21.1 atha bhagavān vṛjiṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caraṅ kuṣṭhagrāmakam anuprāptaḥ kuṣṭhagrāmake viharaty uttareṇa grāmasya śiṃśapāvane ||

Wal 21.2 tatra bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate |

Wal 21.3 itīmāni bhikṣavaḥ śīlāni || ayaṃ samādhiḥ || iyaṃ prajñā || śīlaprabhāvitaḥ samādhiś cirasthitiko bhavati || prajñāparibhāvitaṃ cittaṃ samyag eva vimucyate rāgadveṣamohebhyaḥ ||

Wal 21.4 evaṃ samyaksuvimuktacitta āryaśrāvakaḥ samyag eva prajānāti ||

Wal 21.5 kṣīṇā me jātir uṣitaṃ brahmacaryaṃ kṛtaṃ karaṇīyaṃ nāparam asmād bhavaṃ prajānāmi ||

Hier im Tib. und Skt. Uddāna; cf. MPS p. 495:

kuṣṭha gaṇḍa āmra ca
jambu śūrpa tūla hasti ca ||
grāmau ca vṛjimallau
bhoganagarakaṃ tathā |

Wal 21.6 yathā kuṣṭhagrāmaka evaṃ gaṇḍagrāmako droṇagrāmakaḥ śūrpagrāmaka āmragrāmako jambugrāmako hastigrāmakaḥ ||

Wal 21.7 vṛjigrāmakān mallagrāmakād bhoganagarakam anuprāptaḥ || bhoganagarake viharaty uttareṇa grāmasya śiṃśapāvane ||

Wal 21.8 tatra bhagavān bhikṣūn āmantrayate ||

Wal 21.9 itīmāni bhikṣavaḥ śīlāni pūrvavad yāvad nāparam asmād bhāvaṃ prajānāmi ||

Wal 22.1 tena khalu samayena mahāpṛthivīcālaś cābhūd ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 22.2 athāyuṣmān ānandaḥ sāyāhne pratisaṃlayanād vyutthāya yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagāma || upetya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt ||

Wal 22.3 ekāntasthita āyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 22.4 ko bhadanta hetuḥ kaḥ pratyayo yenaitarhy abhūd mahāpṛthivīcāla ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 22.5 traya ime ānanda hetavas trayaḥ pratyayā mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 22.6 katame trayaḥ ||

Wal 22.7 iyaṃ mahāpṛthivy apsu pratiṣṭhitā pūrvavad yāvac cālayanti ||

Wal 22.8 ayaṃ prathamo hetuḥ prathamaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 22.9 punar aparaṃ bhikṣur maharddhiko bhavati pūrvavad yāvac cālayati ||

Wal 22.10 Nur Tibetisch.

Wal 22.11 ayaṃ dvitīyo hetur dvitīyaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 22.12 punar aparaṃ na cirasyedānīṃ tathāgatasyānupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati || atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavaty ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 22.13 ayaṃ tṛtīyo hetus tṛtīyaḥ pratyayo mahataḥ pṛthivīcālasya ||

Wal 23.1 athāyuṣmān ānando bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 23.2 āscaryādbhutadharmasamanvāgatās tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ || yatredānīṃ na cirasya tathāgatasyānupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau parinirvāṇaṃ bhaviṣyaty atyarthaṃ tasmin samaye mahāpṛthivīcālaś ca bhavaty ulkāpātā diśodāhā antarīkṣe devadundubhayo ’bhinadanti ||

Wal 23.3 evam etad ānanda evam etad ānanda || āścaryādbhutadharmasamanvāgatā eva tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ ||

Wal 23.4 abhijānāmi khalu punar aham anekaśataṃ kṣatriyapariṣadaṃ darśanāyopasaṃkramitum upasaṃkrāntasya ca me yādṛśas teṣām ārohapariṇāho bhavati mamāpi tādṛśa ārohapariṇāho bhavati || yādṛśī teṣāṃ varṇapuṣkalatā bhavati mamāpi tādṛśī varṇapuṣkalatā bhavati || yādṛśī teṣāṃ svaraguptir bhavati mamāpi tādṛśī svaraguptir bhavati ||

Wal 23.5 te yam arthaṃ mantrayanty aham api tam arthaṃ mantrayāmi || te yam arthaṃ na mantrayanty aham api tam arthaṃ na mantrayāmi || uttare vai tān dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayāmi samādāpayāmi samuttejayāmi saṃpraharṣayāmi tato ’ntardhāpayāmi || antarhitasya me na jānanti ka eṣa antarhito devo vā manuṣyo vā ||

Wal 23.6 evam api brāhmaṇapariṣadaṃ gṛhapatipariṣadaṃ śramaṇapariṣadaṃ cāturmahārājikān devāṃs trāyastriṃśān yāmāṃs tuṣitān nirmāṇaratīn parinirmitavaśavartino brahmakāyikān brahmapāriṣadyān brahmapurohitān mahābrahmaṇaḥ parīttābhān apramāṇābhān ābhāsvarān parīttaśubhān apramāṇaśubhāñ śubhakṛtsnān anabhrakān puṇyaprasavān bṛhatphalān abṛhān atapān sudṛśān sudarśanān akaniṣṭhān devān darśanāyopasaṃkramitum

Wal 23.7 upasaṃkrāntasya ca me yādṛśas teṣām ārohapariṇāho bhavati pūrvavad yāvad devo vā manuṣyo vā ||

Wal 23.8 evam āścaryādbhutadharmasamanvāgatās tathāgatā arhantaḥ samyaksaṃbuddhāḥ ||

Wal 24.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 24.2 tasmāt tarhi ta ānanda bhikṣubhiḥ sūtrāntapratisaraṇair bhavitavyaṃ na pudgalapratisaraṇaiḥ ||

Wal 24.3 kathaṃ bhikṣuḥ sūtrāntapratisaraṇo bhavati na pudgalapratisaraṇaḥ ||

Wal 24.4 ihānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṃ vadet ||

Wal 24.5 saṃmukhaṃ me bhagavato ’ntikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam ||

Wal 24.6 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṃ nāvasādayitavyam || anutsāhayitvānavasādayitvā śrotram avadhāya tāni padavyaṃjanāny udgṛhya sūtre ’vatārayitavyaṃ vinaye saṃdarśayitavyaṃ || yadi sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṃdarśyamānāḥ sūtre nāvataranti vinaye na saṃdṛśyante dharmatāṃ ca vilomayanti sa evaṃ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.7 addhāyuṣmann ime dharmā na bhagavatā bhāṣitāḥ || āyuṣmatā vā ime dharmā durgṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṃdarśyamānāḥ sūtre nāvataranti vinaye na saṃdṛśyante dharmatāṃ ca vilomayanti ||

Wal 24.8 nāyaṃ dharmo nāyaṃ vinayo nedaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.9 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṃ vadet ||

Wal 24.10 amuṣminn āvāse mahān bhikṣusaṃghaḥ prativasati sasthaviraḥ sapramokṣaḥ ||

Wal 24.11 saṃmukhaṃ me tasya mahato bhikṣusaṃghasyāntikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanaṃ ||

Wal 24.12 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṃ nāvasādayitavyam || anutsāhayitvānavasādayitvā śrotram avadhāya tāni padavyaṃjanāny udgṛhya sūtre ’vatārayitavyaṃ vinaye saṃdarśayitavyaṃ || yadi sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṃdarśyamānāḥ sūtre nāvataranti vinaye na saṃdṛśyante dharmatāṃ ca vilomayanti sa evaṃ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.13 addhāyuṣmaṃs tena mahatā bhikṣusaṃghena dharmasaṃjñinā ca vinayasaṃjñinā cādharmaś cāvinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || āyuṣmatā vā ime dharmā durgṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṃdarśyamānāḥ sūtre nāvataranti vinaye na saṃdṛśyante dharmatāṃ ca vilomayanti ||

Wal 24.14 nāyaṃ dharmo nāyaṃ vinayo nedaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.15 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṃ vadet ||

Wal 24.16 amuṣminn āvāse saṃbahulā bhikṣavaḥ prativasanti sūtradharā vinayadharā mātṛkādharāḥ ||

Wal 24.17 saṃmukhaṃ me teṣāṃ saṃbahulānāṃ bhikṣūṇām antikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanaṃ

Wal 24.18 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṃ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṃ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.19 addhāyuṣmaṃs tair bhikṣubhir dharmasaṃjñibhiś ca vinayasaṃjñibhiś cādharmaś cāvinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || pūrvavad

Wal 24.20 yāvad iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.21 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṃ vadet ||

Wal 24.22 amuṣminn āvāse bhikṣuḥ prativasati sthaviraḥ … = 24.45

Wal 24.23 saṃmukhaṃ me tasya bhikṣor antikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanaṃ ||

Wal 24.24 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṃ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṃ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.25 addhāyuṣmaṃs tena bhikṣuṇā dharmasaṃjñinā ca vinayasaṃjñinā cādharmaś cāvinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || pūrvavad

Wal 24.26 yāvad iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.27 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṃ vadet ||

Wal 24.28 saṃmukhaṃ me bhagavato ’ntikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam ||

Wal 24.29 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṃ nāvasādayitavyam || anutsāhayitvānavasādayitvā śrotram avadhāya tāni padavyañjanāny udgṛhya sūtre ’vatārayitavyaṃ vinaye sandarśayitavyaṃ || yadi sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye sandarśyamānāḥ sūtre ’vataranti vinaye saṃdṛśyante dharmatāṃ ca na vilomayanti sa evaṃ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.30 addhāyuṣmann ime dharmā bhagavatā bhāṣitāḥ || āyuṣmatā ceme dharmāḥ sugṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṃdarśyamānāḥ sūtre ’vataranti vinaye saṃdṛśyante dharmatāṃ ca na vilomayanti ||

Wal 24.31 ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.32 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṃ vadet ||

Wal 24.33 amuṣminn āvāse mahān bhikṣusaṃghaḥ prativasati sasthaviraḥ sapramokṣaḥ ||

Wal 24.34 saṃmukhaṃ me tasya mahato bhikṣusaṃghasyāntikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam ||

Wal 24.35 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṃ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṃ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.36 addhāyuṣmaṃs tena mahatā bhikṣusaṃghena dharmasaṃjñinā vinayasaṃjñinātra dharmaś ca vinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || āyuṣmatā ceme dharmāḥ sugṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā vinaye saṃdarśyamānāḥ sūtre ’vataranti vinaye na saṃdṛśyante dharmatāñ ca na vilomayanti ||

Wal 24.37 ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.38 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṃ vadet ||

Wal 24.39 amuṣminn āvāse saṃbahulā bhikṣavaḥ prativasanti sūtradharā vinayadharā mātṛkādharāḥ ||

Wal 24.40 saṃmukhaṃ me teṣāṃ saṃbahulānāṃ bhikṣūṇām antikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanaṃ ||

Wal 24.41 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṃ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṃ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.42 addhāyuṣmaṃs tair bhikṣubhir dharmasaṃjñibhiś ca vinayasaṃjñibhiś ca dharmaś ca vinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || āyuṣmatā ceme dharmāḥ sugṛhītās tathā hīme dharmāḥ sūtre ’vatāryamāṇā pūrvavad yāvad

Wal 24.43 ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.44 punar aparam ānanda bhikṣur āgacchet sa evaṃ vadet ||

Wal 24.45 amuṣminn āvāse bhikṣuḥ prativasati sthaviraḥ … = 24.22

Wal 24.46 saṃmukhaṃ me tasya bhikṣor antikāc chrutaṃ saṃmukham udgṛhītam ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam ||

Wal 24.47 tasya bhikṣavas tan notsāhayitavyaṃ pūrvavad yāvat sa evaṃ syād vacanīyaḥ ||

Wal 24.48 addhāyuṣmaṃs tena bhikṣuṇā dharmasaṃjñinā ca vinayasaṃjñinā ca dharmaś ca vinayaś ca bhāṣitaḥ || pūrvavad

Wal 24.49 yāvad iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.50 tatrānanda ye te pūrvakāś catv. … nāyaṃ dharmo nāyaṃ vinayo nedaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā chorayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.51 tatrānanda ye te … ayaṃ dharmo ’yaṃ vinaya idaṃ śāstuḥ śāsanam iti viditvā dhārayitavyāḥ ||

Wal 24.52 evam evānanda bhikṣubhiḥ sūtrāntapratisaraṇair bhavitavyaṃ na pudgalapratisaraṇaiḥ ||

Wal 25 = Sondertext I ST.I. CT 417ff.

Wal 25.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānadam āmantrayate ||

Wal 25.2 āgamayānanda yena rāmagrāmakaḥ || evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 25.3 atha bhagavān krauḍyeṣu janapadeṣu caryāṃ caraṃ rāmagrāmakam anuprāpto rāmagrāmake viharati …

Wal 25.4 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

rāmagrāmake r. .i .. nāma krauḍyaḥ prativasati || sa tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya rāmagrāmake śarīrastūpaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyati śarīrāṇāṃ satkārāya gurukārāya mānanāya pūjanāya arcanāya apacitaye ||

Wal 25.5 sa tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya śarīrastūpapratiṣṭhāpanena … kalpān vinipātaṃ na gamiṣyati devāṃś ca manuṣyāṃś ca sandhāvya saṃsṛtya paścime bhave paścime nikete paścime samucchraye paścime ātmabhāvapratilambhe manuṣyatvaṃ pratilabhya … dharmacaritena keśaśmaśrūṇy avatārya kāṣāyāṇi vastrāṇy ācchādya samyag eva śraddhayāgārād anagārikāṃ pravrajya pratyekāṃ bodhiṃ sākṣīkariṣyati ||

Wal 25.6 viṣṇudvīpe ānanda śubhākṛtsno nāma brāhmaṇaḥ prativasati || so ’pi tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya viṣṇudvīpe śarīrastūpaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya

Wal 25.7 etena śarīrastūpapratiṣṭhāpanena … kalpān vinipātaṃ na gamiṣyati devāṃś ca manuṣyāṃś ca pūrvavad yāvat pratyekāṃ bodhiṃ sākṣīkariṣyati ||

Wal 25.8 kapilavastuny ānanda … buddho nāma śākyaḥ prativasati || so ’pi tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya kapilavastuni śarīrastūpaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya

Wal 25.9 etena śarīrastūpapratiṣṭhāpanena … kalpān vinipātaṃ na gamiṣyati devāṃś ca manuṣyāṃś ca pūrvavad yāvat pratyekāṃ bodhiṃ sākṣīkariṣyati ||

Wal 25.10 rājagṛhe ānanda rājā māgadha ajātaśatrur vaidehīputraḥ prativasati || so ’pi tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya rājagṛhe śarīrastūpaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayiṣyati śarīrāṇāṃ satkārāya gurukārāya mānanāya pūjanāya arcanāya apacitaye ||

Wal 25.11 sa tathāgatasya parinirvṛtasya śarīrastūpapratiṣṭhāpanena … kalpān vinipātaṃ na gamiṣyati devāṃś ca manuṣyāṃś ca pūrvavad yāvat pratyekāṃ bodhiṃ sākṣīkariṣyati ||

Wal 25.12 atha bhagavāṃs tasyāṃ velāyāṃ gāthā babhāṣe ||

Wal 25.13 śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇaniṣkā
jāṃbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṃti ||
ye buddhacaityeṣu prasaṃnacittāḥ
padā vihāre samatikramaṃti |

Wal 25.14 śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇapiṇḍā
jāṃbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṃti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitta
āropayen mṛttikapiṇḍam ekam |

Wal 25.15 śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇamūṭā
jāṃbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṃti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitta
āropayen muktapuṣpasya rāśim |

Wal 25.16 śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇakoṭya
jāṃbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṃti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacittaḥ
pradīpadānaṃ prakaroti vidvān |

Wal 25.17 śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇavāhāḥ
jāṃbūnadā nāsya samā bhavaṃti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitto
mālāvihāraṃ prakaroti vidvān |

Wal 25.18 śataṃ sahasrāṇi suvarṇaparvatāḥ
meroḥ samā nāsya samā bhavaṃti ||
yo buddhacaityeṣu prasannacitta
āropayec chatradhvajaṃ patākam |

Wal 25.19 eṣāho dakṣiṇā proktā
aprameyā tathāgate ||
samudrakalpe saṃbuddhe
sārthavāhe anuttare |

Wal 25.20 tiṣṭhantaṃ pūjayed yaś ca
yaś cāpi parinirvṛtam ||
same cittaprasāde hi
nāsti puṇyaviśeṣatā |

Wal 25.21 na hi citte prasanne ’smim*
svalpā bhavati dakṣiṇā ||
tathāgate vā saṃbuddhe
buddhānāṃ śrāvakeṣu vā |

Wal 25.22 evaṃ hy acintitā buddhā
buddhadharmo ’py acintitaḥ ||
acintite prasādyeha
vipākaḥ syād acintitaḥ |

Wal 25.23 teṣām acintitānām
apratihatadharmacakravartīnām ||
samyaksaṃbuddhānāṃ nālaṃ
guṇapāram adhigantum |

25.24 uddānam* | Cf. Bl. 185 R 6:
.. calakalpā viṣṇudvīpaṃ kapilavastu + rājagṛhaṃ paścimaṃ jñeyam* rāmaś ca ro

Wal 26.1 tatra bhagavān āyuṣmantam ānandam āmantrayate ||

Wal 26.2 āgamayānanda yena pāpāgrāmakaḥ || evaṃ bhadantety āyuṣmān ānando bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣīt ||

Wal 26.3 atha bhagavān malleṣu janapadeṣv anupūrveṇa caryāṃ caran pāpām anuprāptaḥ pāpāyāṃ viharati jalūkāvanaṣaṇḍe ||

Wal 26.4 aśrauṣuḥ pāpīyakā mallā bhagavān malleṣu janapadeṣv anupūrveṇa caryāṃ caran pāpām anuprāptaḥ pāpāyāṃ viharati jalūkāvanaṣaṇḍe ||

Wal 26.5 śrutvā ca punaḥ saṃghāt saṃghaṃ pūgāt pūgaṃ saṃgamya samāgamya pāpāyā niṣkramya yena bhagavāṃs tenopajagmuḥ ||

Wal 26.6 upetya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvaikānte nyaṣīdan || ekāntaniṣaṇṇān bhagavān dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayati samādāpayati samuttejayati saṃpraharṣayati ||

Wal 26.7 tena khalu samayena cundaḥ karmāraputras tasmin samāje sanniṣaṇṇo ’bhūt sannipatitaḥ || atha bhagavān pāpīyakān mallān anekaparyāyeṇa dhārmyā kathayā sandarśayitvā samādāpayitvā samuttejayitvā saṃpraharṣayitvā tūṣṇīm abhūt || atha pāpīyakā mallā bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā prakrāntāḥ ||

Wal 26.8 cundaḥ karmāraputras tatraivāsthāt || atha cundaḥ karmāraputro ’ciraprakrāntān pāpīyakān mallān viditvotthāyāsanād ekāṃsam uttarāsaṅgaṃ kṛtvā yena bhagavāṃs tenāñjaliṃ praṇamya bhagavantam idam avocat ||

Wal 26.9 adhivāsayatu me bhagavāñ śvo bhaktena sārdhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghena ||

Wal 26.10 adhivāsayati bhagavāñ cundasya karmāraputrasya tūṣṇīṃbhāvena ||

Wal 26.11 atha cundaḥ karmāraputro bhagavatas tūṣṇīṃbhāvenādhivāsanāṃ viditvā bhagavato bhāṣitam abhinandyānumodya bhagavatpādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntaḥ ||

Wal 26.12 atha cundaḥ karmāraputras tām eva rātriṃ śuciṃ praṇītaṃ khādanīyabhojanīyaṃ samudānīya kālyam evotthāyāsanakāni prajñapyodakamaṇiṃ pratiṣṭhāpya bhagavato dūtena kālam ārocayati ||

Wal 26.13 samayo bho gautamo sadyo bhaktaṃ yasyedānīṃ bhavāṅ gautamaḥ kālaṃ manyate ||

Wal 26.14 atha bhagavān pūrvāhṇe nivasya pātracīvaram ādāya bhikṣusaṃghaparivṛto bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛto yena cundasya karmāraputrasya bhaktābhisāras tenopajagāma || upetya purastād bhikṣusaṃghasya prajñapta evāsane nyaṣīdat ||

Wal 26.15 atha cundaḥ karmāraputraḥ sukhopaniṣaṇṇaṃ buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ viditvā bhagavantaṃ praṇītena khādanīyena lohakaroṭakāt svahastaṃ santarpayati saṃpravārayati || bhikṣusaṃghaṃ ca śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ santarpayati saṃpravārayati ||

Wal 26.16 tena samayena anyatamaḥ pāpabhikṣur lohakaroṭakaṃ kakṣeṇāpahṛtavāṃs taṃ khalu pāpabhikṣuṃ bhagavān adrākṣīc cundaś ca buddhānubhāvena ||

Wal 26.17 atha cundaḥ karmāraputro buddhapramukhaṃ bhikṣusaṃghaṃ śucinā praṇītena khādanīyabhojanīyena svahastaṃ santarpayitvā saṃpravārayitvā bhagavantaṃ bhuktavantaṃ viditvā dhautahastam apanītapātraṃ nīcatarakam āsanaṃ gṛhītvā bhagavataḥ purato niṣadya bhagavantaṃ gāthābhir gītābhiḥ papraccha ||

Wal 26.30 dadataḥ puṇyaṃ pra + + +
